## Kullanıcı

1	# AGENTS.md — Üretim Performans Takip Uygulaması (MAGNA Case Study)
2	
3	> **Bu dosya AI kod asistanları için TEK KAYNAK (canonical) bağlamdır.** Açık standart `AGENTS.md`
4	> formatındadır; **MiniMax** bunu doğrudan okur.
5	>
6	> **SENKRON:** `CLAUDE.md` bu dosyanın kopyasıdır (Claude Code için). İçeriği yalnız bu dosyada
7	> değiştir, sonra **`make ai-sync`** çalıştır → `CLAUDE.md` güncellenir. Detay:
8	> [`.docs/shared/conventions/ai-assistants.md`](.docs/shared/conventions/ai-assistants.md).
9	>
10	> Detaylar için `.docs/`, plan için `.roadmap/`.
11	
12	---
13	
14	## 1. Proje Nedir?
15	
16	Otomotiv yan sanayi (enjeksiyon kalıplama) hattı için **üretim performans ve OEE takip** web
17	uygulaması. MES'ten gelen `.csv` üretim raporlarını:
18	
19	1. Sisteme **import** eder (CSV → SQLite)
20	2. **Veri kalite validasyonu** yapar (hatalı/şüpheli kayıtları tespit, sınıflandır, raporla, düzelt) ← **kritik**
21	3. Filtreleme + **OEE dashboard** ile raporlar
22	4. **Sadece temiz/onaylı** veriyi harici REST API'ye gönderir ← **2. kritik**
23	
24	İşe alım case study'si (MAGNA). Aday: **Umut Arda Özdeş**. Süre: **2 iş günü**. Teslim: GitHub repo
25	`umut-arda-ozdes-uretim-takip-case` + e-posta `tunahan.ozturk@magna.com`.
26	
27	## 2. Kritik Kurallar (asla ihlal etme)
28	
29	1. **Veriyi "temiz" varsayma.** Gerçek MES verisi gibi kalite sorunları + mantıksal
30	   tutarsızlıklar var. Değerlendirmenin merkezi bunları yakalamaktır (**%25**).
31	2. **Sadece valide + onaylı kayıtlar hedef API'ye gider.** Hatalı kaydın hedefe ulaşmaması en
32	   kritik gereksinimlerden biridir.
33	3. **Secret koda gömülmez.** `TARGET_API_KEY` yalnız `.env`'den okunur. `.env` git'e girmez;
34	   `.env.example` paylaşılır.
35	4. **API gönderimi idempotent.** Aynı (tarih, vardiya) iki kez → duplicate yok. Retry/backoff zorunlu.
36	5. **Her hata tipini gerekçe + örnekle belgele.** Yanlış pozitif puan kaybettirir → reject (yüksek
37	   güven) vs warn (sezgisel) ayrımı.
38	6. **3 komuttan az kurulum.** `make setup && make dev` çalışmalı.
39	7. **AI kullanımı şeffaf.** Tüm AI sohbet/prompt'lar `ai_usage/` altında (case §8 — %5).
40	
41	## 3. Stack & Gerekçe (detay: `.docs/shared/decisions/`)
42	
43	| Katman | Seçim |
44	|--------|-------|
45	| Frontend | **Next.js (App Router) + TypeScript** |
46	| UI | **shadcn/ui + Tailwind** (özel token'lar, `tailwind.config.ts`) |
47	| Charts / State | Recharts · TanStack Query (server) + Zustand (UI) |
48	| Backend | **FastAPI** (Pydantic validasyon + otomatik OpenAPI) |
49	| DB | **SQLite (zorunlu) + SQLAlchemy** |
50	| HTTP | httpx + tenacity (retry/backoff) |
51	
52	> Frontend secret tutmaz. Hedef API çağrısı (X-Production-Key) **sadece FastAPI**'de.
53	> Akış: Browser → Next.js → FastAPI → Hedef API.
54	
55	## 4. Proje Yapısı (detay: `.docs/shared/architecture/monorepo.md`)
56	
57	```
58	backend/   FastAPI backend  (app/features: ingestion, validation, analytics, records, sync)
59	frontend/  Next.js frontend (src/features: import, dashboard, records, validation, sync)
60	db/        SQLite veritabanı (app.db + README)   data/  production_data.csv (commit edilir)
61	ai_usage/  AI logları (§8)   scripts/ yardımcılar   .docs/ doküman   .roadmap/ plan + CHECKLIST
62	Makefile · README.md · .env.example · AGENTS.md (MiniMax) + CLAUDE.md
63	```
64	
65	## 5. Komutlar (Makefile)
66	
67	```bash
68	make setup      # .env kopyala + bağımlılıklar (api venv + web npm)
69	make dev        # api (:8000) + web (:3000)
70	make db-init    # SQLite şema      make seed   # CSV import
71	make test       # testler (özellikle validation)
72	make lint / format / check
73	make ai-sync    # AGENTS.md → CLAUDE.md (senkron)
74	make hooks      # git hook'ları kur (secret koruması + ai-sync)
75	```
76	Portlar: web **:3000**, api **:8000** (Swagger `/docs`).
77	
78	## 6. Domain Bilgisi (detay: `.docs/shared/domain/`)
79	
80	- **OEE = A × P × Q / 10000** (yüzde). A = Çalışma/(Çalışma+Plansız Duruş);
81	  P = ideal hıza karşı; Q = (Üretilen−Hatalı)/Üretilen.
82	- Kaynak: `production_data.csv` — 2.117 satır, 18 kolon, 5–25 Kasım 2025.
83	- 18 kolon → `.docs/shared/domain/data-dictionary.md`. Vardiya: 1 Sabah / 2 Öğle / 3 Gece.
84	
85	## 7. Hedef API (detay: `.docs/shared/api-contract/target-api.md`)
86	
87	- `POST {TARGET_API_URL}/api/v1/submit`, header `X-Production-Key`, body JSON.
88	- Gönderim **(tarih, vardiya) bazında agrege**: `{machine_count, total_production_units, oe_value, shift, production_date}`.
89	- Hatalar: 401 (key), 422 (detail'e bak), 429 (rate limit 1dk), 413 (>10KB).
90	- Idempotency key + retry/backoff → `app/features/sync/`. Tam dok: `http://89.252.189.91:8983/docs-guide`.
91	
92	## 8. Konvansiyonlar
93	
94	- **Dil:** Dokümanlar Türkçe; kod/identifier İngilizce.
95	- **Validasyon kuralları** `app/features/validation/rules/` (her kural ayrı + test). Katalog
96	  (kaynak doğruluk): `.docs/shared/domain/validation-rules.md`.
97	- İş mantığı service/feature'da; router/component ince.
98	- **Stil:** sadece Tailwind semantic token'ları (`.docs/web/theme.md`). Hardcoded renk yok.
99	- **Plan değişince** `.roadmap/CHECKLIST.md`'i güncelle (yapıldı/yapılmadı).
100	- Tip ipuçları zorunlu (Python public fn'ler); `any` yasak (TS).
101	- **Skill'ler** `.claude/skills/` (SKILL.md): tekrarlayan işler için (validasyon kuralı/feature ekleme, kalite kontrolleri).
102	- **Feature izolasyonu:** feature'lar birbirini import etmez; ortak kod `shared`'a. ESLint (`boundaries`) zorunlu kılar. Bkz. `.docs/web/feature-architecture.md`.
103	- **Yasaklar (lint zorunlu):** `.docs/shared/conventions/prohibitions.md` — `any` yok, doğrudan `process.env` yok, cross-feature import yok, hardcoded renk yok.
104	
105	## 9. Yapma / Dikkat
106	
107	Kaçınılması gerekenler:
108	- Hatalı/şüpheli kaydı hedef API'ye gönderme.
109	- Secret'ı koda, log'a veya frontend'e koyma.
110	- `data/production_data.csv`'i .gitignore'lama (runtime DB ise gitignore'lu).
111	- Gerekçesiz/agresif validasyon kuralı eklemek (yanlış pozitif).
112	
113	Yapılması gerekenler:
114	- Tespit edilen her hatayı gerekçe + örnekle belgele.
115	- "Yapamadıklarını" README'de dürüstçe yaz.
116	
117	## 10. Bellek (Memory)
118	
119	- Kalıcı çalışma belleği `.ai/memory/`: `project.md` (curated kararlar/durum) + `tasks.md` (görev log).
120	- Görev tamamlanınca `tasks.md`'e tek satır ekle; kalıcı karar/öğreni varsa `project.md`'i güncelle.
121	- Yeni oturuma başlarken önce bu ikisini oku. MiniMax: `MINIMAX_MEMORY_PATH=.ai/memory`.
122	- **Her görev sonunda:** `tasks.md`'i güncelle + `make ai-export` ile transcript'i tazele (§8; idempotent). `make ai-backup` bunu çağırıp `ai_usage/`'i commit eder (push yapmaz; push kullanıcıya bırakılır).
123	- **Transcript kaynakları (`make ai-export` hepsini tarar):** Claude Code (VS Code + CLI) `~/.claude/projects/<proje>/*.jsonl`; MiniMax (opencode CLI) `~/.local/share/opencode/opencode.db` (SQLite); eski MiniMax JSONL `~/.minimax/sessions`. Bu projeye ait **tüm** oturumlar her seferinde yedeklenir (sadece sonuncusu değil).
124

## Kullanıcı

1	"use client";
2	
3	import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
4	import { api } from "@/lib/api";
5	import { queryKeys } from "@/lib/query-keys";
6	import type {
7	  KpiCards,
8	  OeeTrendPoint,
9	  ProblemShiftRow,
10	  QualityDistributionBucket,
11	  RecentRecordRow,
12	  ShiftComparisonRow,
13	  StationRankingRow,
14	  TopStationRow,
15	} from "./types";
16	
17	export function useKpis() {
18	  return useQuery({
19	    queryKey: queryKeys.analytics.kpis(),
20	    queryFn: () => api.get<KpiCards>("/api/v1/analytics/kpis"),
21	  });
22	}
23	
24	export function useKpisPeriod(start: string | null, end: string | null) {
25	  const q = new URLSearchParams();
26	  if (start) q.set("start", start);
27	  if (end) q.set("end", end);
28	  const qs = q.toString();
29	  return useQuery({
30	    queryKey: ["analytics", "kpis", "period", start, end] as const,
31	    queryFn: () =>
32	      api.get<KpiCards>(`/api/v1/analytics/kpis${qs ? `?${qs}` : ""}`),
33	  });
34	}
35	
36	export function useOeeTrend(days: number = 21) {
37	  return useQuery({
38	    queryKey: [...queryKeys.analytics.oeeTrend(null), days] as const,
39	    queryFn: () => api.get<OeeTrendPoint[]>(`/api/v1/analytics/oee-trend?days=${days}`),
40	  });
41	}
42	
43	export function useShiftComparison() {
44	  return useQuery({
45	    queryKey: queryKeys.analytics.shiftComparison(null),
46	    queryFn: () => api.get<ShiftComparisonRow[]>("/api/v1/analytics/shift-comparison"),
47	  });
48	}
49	
50	export function useStationRanking(limit: number = 10) {
51	  return useQuery({
52	    queryKey: [...queryKeys.analytics.stationRanking(null), limit] as const,
53	    queryFn: () =>
54	      api.get<StationRankingRow[]>(`/api/v1/analytics/station-ranking?limit=${limit}`),
55	  });
56	}
57	
58	export function useQualityDistribution() {
59	  return useQuery({
60	    queryKey: queryKeys.analytics.qualityDistribution(null),
61	    queryFn: () => api.get<QualityDistributionBucket[]>("/api/v1/analytics/quality-distribution"),
62	  });
63	}
64	
65	export function useRecentRecords(batchId: number | null, limit: number = 20) {
66	  const q = new URLSearchParams();
67	  if (batchId !== null) q.set("batch_id", String(batchId));
68	  q.set("limit", String(limit));
69	  return useQuery({
70	    queryKey: queryKeys.analytics.recentRecords(batchId),
71	    queryFn: () => api.get<RecentRecordRow[]>(`/api/v1/analytics/recent-records?${q.toString()}`),
72	  });
73	}
74	
75	export function useTopStations(batchId: number | null, limit: number = 10) {
76	  const q = new URLSearchParams();
77	  if (batchId !== null) q.set("batch_id", String(batchId));
78	  q.set("limit", String(limit));
79	  return useQuery({
80	    queryKey: queryKeys.analytics.topStations(batchId),
81	    queryFn: () => api.get<TopStationRow[]>(`/api/v1/analytics/top-stations?${q.toString()}`),
82	  });
83	}
84	
85	export function useProblemShifts(batchId: number | null, limit: number = 20) {
86	  const q = new URLSearchParams();
87	  if (batchId !== null) q.set("batch_id", String(batchId));
88	  q.set("limit", String(limit));
89	  return useQuery({
90	    queryKey: queryKeys.analytics.problemShifts(batchId),
91	    queryFn: () => api.get<ProblemShiftRow[]>(`/api/v1/analytics/problem-shifts?${q.toString()}`),
92	  });
93	}
94

## Kullanıcı

1	"use client";
2	
3	import { useState } from "react";
4	import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
5	import { useActiveBatch } from "@/hooks/useActiveBatch";
6	import { DashboardHeader } from "./DashboardHeader";
7	import { KpiCardGrid } from "./KpiCardGrid";
8	import { OeeTrendChart } from "./OeeTrendChart";
9	import { ProblemShiftsTable } from "./ProblemShiftsTable";
10	import { QualityDistributionChart } from "./QualityDistributionChart";
11	import { RecentRecordsTable } from "./RecentRecordsTable";
12	import { ShiftComparisonChart } from "./ShiftComparisonChart";
13	import { StationRankingChart } from "./StationRankingChart";
14	import { TopStationsTable } from "./TopStationsTable";
15	
16	export function DashboardPage() {
17	  const active = useActiveBatch();
18	  const batchId: number | null = active.data?.id ?? null;
19	  const [tab, setTab] = useState("recent");
20	
21	  return (
22	    <main className="container mx-auto space-y-6 py-8">
23	      <DashboardHeader />
24	
25	      <KpiCardGrid />
26	
27	      <section className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 lg:grid-cols-2">
28	        <OeeTrendChart />
29	        <ShiftComparisonChart />
30	      </section>
31	
32	      <section className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 lg:grid-cols-2">
33	        <StationRankingChart />
34	        <QualityDistributionChart />
35	      </section>
36	
37	      <Tabs value={tab} onValueChange={setTab}>
38	        <TabsList>
39	          <TabsTrigger value="recent">Son Kayıtlar</TabsTrigger>
40	          <TabsTrigger value="top">Top İstasyonlar</TabsTrigger>
41	          <TabsTrigger value="problems">Sorunlu Vardiyalar</TabsTrigger>
42	        </TabsList>
43	        <TabsContent value="recent">
44	          <RecentRecordsTable batchId={batchId} />
45	        </TabsContent>
46	        <TabsContent value="top">
47	          <TopStationsTable batchId={batchId} />
48	        </TabsContent>
49	        <TabsContent value="problems">
50	          <ProblemShiftsTable batchId={batchId} />
51	        </TabsContent>
52	      </Tabs>
53	    </main>
54	  );
55	}
56

## Kullanıcı

1	"use client";
2	
3	import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
4	import {
5	  flexRender,
6	  getCoreRowModel,
7	  getSortedRowModel,
8	  useReactTable,
9	  type ColumnDef,
10	  type SortingState,
11	} from "@tanstack/react-table";
12	import { Inbox } from "lucide-react";
13	import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
14	import { oeeColorClass } from "@/lib/utils";
15	import { useRecentRecords } from "./useDashboardData";
16	import type { RecentRecordRow } from "./types";
17	
18	const SHIFT_LABELS: Record<number, string> = { 1: "Sabah", 2: "Öğle", 3: "Gece" };
19	
20	const fmtDate = (s: string | null): string => (s ? s : "—");
21	const fmtNum = (n: number | null | undefined): string =>
22	  n === null || n === undefined ? "—" : n.toLocaleString("tr-TR");
23	
24	export interface RecentRecordsTableProps {
25	  batchId: number | null;
26	}
27	
28	export function RecentRecordsTable({ batchId }: RecentRecordsTableProps) {
29	  const q = useRecentRecords(batchId, 20);
30	  const [sorting, setSorting] = useState<SortingState>([]);
31	  const data = q.data ?? [];
32	
33	  const columns = useMemo<ColumnDef<RecentRecordRow>[]>(
34	    () => [
35	      {
36	        accessorKey: "prod_date",
37	        header: "Tarih",
38	        cell: (info) => (
39	          <span className="font-mono text-xs">{fmtDate(info.getValue<string | null>())}</span>
40	        ),
41	      },
42	      {
43	        accessorKey: "shift",
44	        header: "Vardiya",
45	        cell: (info) => {
46	          const v = info.getValue<number | null>();
47	          return v === null ? "—" : (SHIFT_LABELS[v] ?? `Vardiya ${v}`);
48	        },
49	      },
50	      {
51	        accessorKey: "station_name",
52	        header: "İstasyon",
53	        cell: (info) => info.getValue<string | null>() ?? "—",
54	      },
55	      {
56	        accessorKey: "stock_name",
57	        header: "Stok",
58	        cell: (info) => (
59	          <span className="font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">
60	            {info.getValue<string | null>() ?? "—"}
61	          </span>
62	        ),
63	      },
64	      {
65	        accessorKey: "oee",
66	        header: "OEE",
67	        cell: (info) => {
68	          const v = info.getValue<number | null>();
69	          return v === null ? (
70	            "—"
71	          ) : (
72	            <span className={`tabular-nums ${oeeColorClass(v)}`}>{v.toFixed(1)}%</span>
73	          );
74	        },
75	      },
76	      {
77	        accessorKey: "produced_qty",
78	        header: "Üretim",
79	        cell: (info) => (
80	          <span className="tabular-nums">{fmtNum(info.getValue<number | null>())}</span>
81	        ),
82	      },
83	      {
84	        accessorKey: "scrap_qty",
85	        header: "Fire",
86	        cell: (info) => {
87	          const v = info.getValue<number | null>();
88	          return (
89	            <span className={`tabular-nums ${v && v > 0 ? "text-oee-low" : ""}`}>
90	              {fmtNum(v)}
91	            </span>
92	          );
93	        },
94	      },
95	      {
96	        accessorKey: "status",
97	        header: "Durum",
98	        cell: (info) => (
99	          <span className="text-xs uppercase text-muted-foreground">
100	            {info.getValue<string>()}
101	          </span>
102	        ),
103	      },
104	    ],
105	    [],
106	  );
107	
108	  const table = useReactTable({
109	    data,
110	    columns,
111	    state: { sorting },
112	    onSortingChange: setSorting,
113	    getCoreRowModel: getCoreRowModel(),
114	    getSortedRowModel: getSortedRowModel(),
115	  });
116	
117	  return (
118	    <div className="overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-card text-card-foreground">
119	      <table className="w-full text-sm">
120	        <thead>
121	          {table.getHeaderGroups().map((hg) => (
122	            <tr key={hg.id} className="border-b bg-muted/40 text-left text-xs uppercase text-muted-foreground">
123	              {hg.headers.map((h) => (
124	                <th
125	                  key={h.id}
126	                  className="cursor-pointer select-none p-2"
127	                  onClick={h.column.getToggleSortingHandler()}
128	                >
129	                  {flexRender(h.column.columnDef.header, h.getContext())}
130	                  {h.column.getIsSorted() === "asc"
131	                    ? " ▲"
132	                    : h.column.getIsSorted() === "desc"
133	                      ? " ▼"
134	                      : ""}
135	                </th>
136	              ))}
137	            </tr>
138	          ))}
139	        </thead>
140	        <tbody>
141	          {q.isLoading ? (
142	            Array.from({ length: 6 }).map((_, i) => (
143	              <tr key={`s_${i}`} className="border-b">
144	                <td colSpan={columns.length} className="p-2">
145	                  <Skeleton className="h-6 w-full" />
146	                </td>
147	              </tr>
148	            ))
149	          ) : table.getRowModel().rows.length === 0 ? (
150	            <tr>
151	              <td colSpan={columns.length} className="p-8">
152	                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
153	                  <Inbox className="h-8 w-8 opacity-60" />
154	                  <p>Veri yok</p>
155	                </div>
156	              </td>
157	            </tr>
158	          ) : (
159	            table.getRowModel().rows.map((row) => (
160	              <tr key={row.id} className="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/40">
161	                {row.getVisibleCells().map((cell) => (
162	                  <td key={cell.id} className="p-2 align-top">
163	                    {flexRender(cell.column.columnDef.cell, cell.getContext())}
164	                  </td>
165	                ))}
166	              </tr>
167	            ))
168	          )}
169	        </tbody>
170	      </table>
171	    </div>
172	  );
173	}
174

## Asistan

The table components look fine. The issue is likely the backend endpoints. Let me check the backend analytics router.

27	def _parse_filters(
28	    start: dt.date | None,
29	    end: dt.date | None,
30	    shift: list[int] | None,
31	    station_name: list[str] | None,
32	    stock_name: str | None,
33	    oee_min: float | None,
34	    oee_max: float | None,
35	    validation_status: list[str] | None,
36	    has_issues: bool | None,
37	) -> RecordFilter:
38	    return RecordFilter(
39	        prod_date_range=DateRange(start=start, end=end) if (start or end) else None,
40	        shift=shift or [],
41	        station_name=station_name or [],
42	        stock_name=stock_name,
43	        oee_range=OeeRange(min=oee_min, max=oee_max) if (oee_min is not None or oee_max is not None) else None,
44	        validation_status=validation_status or [],
45	        has_issues=has_issues,
46	    )

## Kullanıcı

1	"""Analytics service — OEE recompute + filtre-aware agregasyonlar."""
2	from __future__ import annotations
3	
4	import datetime as dt
5	from collections.abc import Sequence
6	from typing import Any
7	
8	from sqlalchemy import case, func, or_, select
9	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
10	
11	from app.db import models
12	from app.features.records.schemas import DateRange, RecordFilter
13	from app.features.records.service import _apply_filter, _build_issue_subquery
14	
15	# OEE = bileşenlerden yeniden hesaplanmış `oee_recomputed` (bkz. app.core.oee),
16	# basit ortalama, TÜM kayıtlar üzerinden (hacim metrikleriyle aynı kapsam).
17	# Hesaplanamayan/boş kayıtlar SQL AVG tarafından dışlanır.
18	_QUALITY_BUCKETS: tuple[tuple[float, float, str], ...] = (
19	    (0.0, 10.0, "0-10"),
20	    (10.0, 20.0, "10-20"),
21	    (20.0, 30.0, "20-30"),
22	    (30.0, 40.0, "30-40"),
23	    (40.0, 50.0, "40-50"),
24	    (50.0, 60.0, "50-60"),
25	    (60.0, 70.0, "60-70"),
26	    (70.0, 80.0, "70-80"),
27	    (80.0, 90.0, "80-90"),
28	    (90.0, 100.01, "90-100"),
29	)
30	
31	
32	def _safe_avg(values: Sequence[float | None]) -> float | None:
33	    cleaned: list[float] = [float(v) for v in values if v is not None]
34	    if not cleaned:
35	        return None
36	    return sum(cleaned) / len(cleaned)
37	
38	
39	def _avg_oee_and_counts(
40	    db: Session,
41	    flt: RecordFilter,
42	) -> tuple[float | None, int, int, int, int]:
43	    """Ortalama OEE (basit ortalama, `oee_recomputed` üzerinden) + statü sayıları.
44	
45	    OEE bileşenlerden yeniden hesaplanıp [0,100]'e clamp'lendiği için (bkz.
46	    `app.core.oee`) artık garbage yok; ham `oee` kolonu yerine `oee_recomputed`
47	    kullanılır. SQL AVG, NULL (hesaplanamayan / boş kayıt) değerleri otomatik
48	    dışlar. Sayımlar tüm kayıtlardan gelir (hacim metrikleriyle aynı kapsam).
49	    """
50	    issue_subq = _build_issue_subquery()
51	    stmt = select(
52	        func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).label("avg_oee"),
53	        func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
54	        func.sum(case((models.ProductionRecord.status == "valid", 1), else_=0)).label("v_cnt"),
55	        func.sum(case((models.ProductionRecord.status == "suspect", 1), else_=0)).label("s_cnt"),
56	        func.sum(case((models.ProductionRecord.status == "rejected", 1), else_=0)).label("r_cnt"),
57	    )
58	    stmt = _apply_filter(stmt, flt, issue_subq=issue_subq)
59	    row = db.execute(stmt).one()
60	    avg: float | None = float(row.avg_oee) if row.avg_oee is not None else None
61	    return avg, int(row.cnt or 0), int(row.v_cnt or 0), int(row.s_cnt or 0), int(row.r_cnt or 0)
62	
63	
64	def _sum_production_scrap_down(
65	    db: Session,
66	    flt: RecordFilter,
67	) -> tuple[int, int, float]:
68	    issue_subq = _build_issue_subquery()
69	    stmt = select(
70	        func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
71	        func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty), 0).label("s"),
72	        func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.down_time), 0.0).label("d"),
73	    )
74	    stmt = _apply_filter(stmt, flt, issue_subq=issue_subq)
75	    row = db.execute(stmt).one()
76	    return int(row.p or 0), int(row.s or 0), float(row.d or 0.0)
77	
78	
79	def kpis(db: Session, flt: RecordFilter) -> dict[str, Any]:
80	    avg_oee, cnt, v_cnt, s_cnt, r_cnt = _avg_oee_and_counts(db, flt)
81	    p, s, d = _sum_production_scrap_down(db, flt)
82	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import KpiCards
83	    return KpiCards(
84	        avg_oee=avg_oee,
85	        total_production=p,
86	        total_scrap=s,
87	        total_down_time_minutes=d,
88	        record_count=cnt,
89	        valid_count=v_cnt,
90	        suspect_count=s_cnt,
91	        rejected_count=r_cnt,
92	    ).model_dump()
93	
94	
95	def oee_trend(
96	    db: Session,
97	    flt: RecordFilter,
98	    days: int = 21,
99	) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
100	    end_date: dt.date | None = None
101	    if flt.prod_date_range and flt.prod_date_range.end:
102	        end_date = flt.prod_date_range.end
103	    else:
104	        # Tarih filtresi yoksa "bugün"e değil veri setindeki en son üretim
105	        # tarihine sabitle — veri tarihsel olabilir (örn. seed = Kasım 2025).
106	        max_stmt = _apply_filter(
107	            select(func.max(models.ProductionRecord.prod_date)),
108	            flt,
109	            issue_subq=_build_issue_subquery(),
110	        )
111	        end_date = db.execute(max_stmt).scalar() or dt.date.today()
112	    start = end_date - dt.timedelta(days=days - 1)
113	    range_flt = RecordFilter(
114	        prod_date_range=DateRange(start=start, end=end_date),
115	        shift=list(flt.shift),
116	        station_name=list(flt.station_name),
117	        stock_name=flt.stock_name,
118	        oee_range=flt.oee_range,
119	        validation_status=list(flt.validation_status),
120	        has_issues=flt.has_issues,
121	    )
122	    issue_subq = _build_issue_subquery()
123	    stmt = (
124	        select(
125	            models.ProductionRecord.prod_date.label("d"),
126	            func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).label("avg_oee"),
127	            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
128	            func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
129	        )
130	        .group_by(models.ProductionRecord.prod_date)
131	        .order_by(models.ProductionRecord.prod_date.asc())
132	    )
133	    stmt = _apply_filter(stmt, range_flt, issue_subq=issue_subq)
134	    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
135	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import OeeTrendPoint
136	    out: list[OeeTrendPoint] = []
137	    for r in rows:
138	        out.append(
139	            OeeTrendPoint(
140	                prod_date=r.d,
141	                avg_oee=float(r.avg_oee) if r.avg_oee is not None else None,
142	                total_production=int(r.p or 0),
143	                record_count=int(r.cnt or 0),
144	            )
145	        )
146	    return [o.model_dump() for o in out]
147	
148	
149	def shift_comparison(
150	    db: Session,
151	    flt: RecordFilter,
152	) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
153	    issue_subq = _build_issue_subquery()
154	    stmt = (
155	        select(
156	            models.ProductionRecord.shift.label("s"),
157	            func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).label("avg_oee"),
158	            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
159	            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty), 0).label("sc"),
160	            func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
161	        )
162	        .where(models.ProductionRecord.shift.isnot(None))
163	        .group_by(models.ProductionRecord.shift)
164	        .order_by(models.ProductionRecord.shift.asc())
165	    )
166	    stmt = _apply_filter(stmt, flt, issue_subq=issue_subq)
167	    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
168	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import ShiftComparisonRow
169	    out: list[ShiftComparisonRow] = []
170	    for r in rows:
171	        out.append(
172	            ShiftComparisonRow(
173	                shift=int(r.s),
174	                avg_oee=float(r.avg_oee) if r.avg_oee is not None else None,
175	                total_production=int(r.p or 0),
176	                total_scrap=int(r.sc or 0),
177	                record_count=int(r.cnt or 0),
178	            )
179	        )
180	    return [o.model_dump() for o in out]
181	
182	
183	def station_ranking(
184	    db: Session,
185	    flt: RecordFilter,
186	    limit: int = 10,
187	) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
188	    issue_subq = _build_issue_subquery()
189	    stmt = (
190	        select(
191	            models.ProductionRecord.station_name.label("st"),
192	            func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).label("avg_oee"),
193	            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
194	            func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
195	        )
196	        .where(models.ProductionRecord.station_name.isnot(None))
197	        .group_by(models.ProductionRecord.station_name)
198	        .order_by(func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).desc())
199	        .limit(limit)
200	    )
201	    stmt = _apply_filter(stmt, flt, issue_subq=issue_subq)
202	    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
203	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import StationRankingRow
204	    out: list[StationRankingRow] = []
205	    for r in rows:
206	        out.append(
207	            StationRankingRow(
208	                station_name=str(r.st),
209	                avg_oee=float(r.avg_oee) if r.avg_oee is not None else None,
210	                total_production=int(r.p or 0),
211	                record_count=int(r.cnt or 0),
212	            )
213	        )
214	    return [o.model_dump() for o in out]
215	
216	
217	def quality_distribution(
218	    db: Session,
219	    flt: RecordFilter,
220	) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
221	    issue_subq = _build_issue_subquery()
222	    stmt = select(
223	        models.ProductionRecord.quality.label("q"),
224	        func.coalesce(models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty, 0).label("sc"),
225	    ).where(models.ProductionRecord.quality.isnot(None))
226	    stmt = _apply_filter(stmt, flt, issue_subq=issue_subq)
227	    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
228	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import QualityDistributionBucket
229	    counts: dict[tuple[float, float, str], tuple[int, int]] = dict.fromkeys(_QUALITY_BUCKETS, (0, 0))
230	    for r in rows:
231	        qv = float(r.q)
232	        for low, high, label in _QUALITY_BUCKETS:
233	            if low <= qv < high:
234	                key = (low, high, label)
235	                c, s = counts[key]
236	                counts[key] = (c + 1, s + int(r.sc or 0))
237	                break
238	    out: list[QualityDistributionBucket] = []
239	    for (low, high, label), (c, s) in counts.items():
240	        out.append(
241	            QualityDistributionBucket(
242	                bucket_label=label,
243	                bucket_start=low,
244	                bucket_end=high,
245	                record_count=c,
246	                total_scrap=s,
247	            )
248	        )
249	    return [o.model_dump() for o in out]
250	
251	
252	def recent_records(
253	    db: Session,
254	    batch_id: int | None = None,
255	    limit: int = 20,
256	) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
257	    stmt = select(
258	        models.ProductionRecord.id,
259	        models.ProductionRecord.prod_date,
260	        models.ProductionRecord.shift,
261	        models.ProductionRecord.station_name,
262	        models.ProductionRecord.stock_name,
263	        models.ProductionRecord.oee,
264	        models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty,
265	        models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty,
266	        models.ProductionRecord.status,
267	        models.ProductionRecord.created_at,
268	    )
269	    if batch_id is not None:
270	        stmt = stmt.where(models.ProductionRecord.import_batch_id == batch_id)
271	    stmt = stmt.order_by(
272	        models.ProductionRecord.created_at.desc(),
273	        models.ProductionRecord.id.desc(),
274	    ).limit(limit)
275	    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
276	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import RecentRecordOut
277	    return [
278	        RecentRecordOut(
279	            id=int(r.id),
280	            prod_date=r.prod_date,
281	            shift=int(r.shift) if r.shift is not None else None,
282	            station_name=r.station_name,
283	            stock_name=r.stock_name,
284	            oee=float(r.oee) if r.oee is not None else None,
285	            produced_qty=int(r.produced_qty) if r.produced_qty is not None else None,
286	            scrap_qty=int(r.scrap_qty) if r.scrap_qty is not None else None,
287	            status=str(r.status),
288	            created_at=r.created_at,
289	        ).model_dump()
290	        for r in rows
291	    ]
292	
293	
294	def top_stations(
295	    db: Session,
296	    batch_id: int | None = None,
297	    limit: int = 10,
298	) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
299	    stmt = (
300	        select(
301	            models.ProductionRecord.station_name.label("st"),
302	            func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).label("avg_oee"),
303	            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
304	            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty), 0).label("sc"),
305	            func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
306	        )
307	        .where(models.ProductionRecord.station_name.isnot(None))
308	        .group_by(models.ProductionRecord.station_name)
309	        .order_by(func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed).desc())
310	        .limit(limit)
311	    )
312	    if batch_id is not None:
313	        stmt = stmt.where(models.ProductionRecord.import_batch_id == batch_id)
314	    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
315	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import TopStationOut
316	    return [
317	        TopStationOut(
318	            station_name=str(r.st),
319	            avg_oee=float(r.avg_oee) if r.avg_oee is not None else None,
320	            total_production=int(r.p or 0),
321	            total_scrap=int(r.sc or 0),
322	            record_count=int(r.cnt or 0),
323	        ).model_dump()
324	        for r in rows
325	    ]
326	
327	
328	def problem_shifts(
329	    db: Session,
330	    batch_id: int | None = None,
331	    limit: int = 20,
332	) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
333	    avg_oee_expr = func.avg(models.ProductionRecord.oee_recomputed)
334	    rejected_count_expr = func.sum(
335	        case((models.ProductionRecord.status == "rejected", 1), else_=0)
336	    )
337	    stmt = (
338	        select(
339	            models.ProductionRecord.prod_date.label("d"),
340	            models.ProductionRecord.shift.label("s"),
341	            models.ProductionRecord.station_name.label("st"),
342	            avg_oee_expr.label("avg_oee"),
343	            rejected_count_expr.label("rejected_count"),
344	            func.coalesce(func.sum(models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty), 0).label("p"),
345	            func.count(models.ProductionRecord.id).label("cnt"),
346	        )
347	        .where(models.ProductionRecord.shift.isnot(None))
348	        .group_by(
349	            models.ProductionRecord.prod_date,
350	            models.ProductionRecord.shift,
351	            models.ProductionRecord.station_name,
352	        )
353	        .having(
354	            or_(
355	                avg_oee_expr < 60,
356	                rejected_count_expr > 0,
357	            )
358	        )
359	        .order_by(avg_oee_expr.asc())
360	        .limit(limit)
361	    )
362	    if batch_id is not None:
363	        stmt = stmt.where(models.ProductionRecord.import_batch_id == batch_id)
364	    rows = db.execute(stmt).all()
365	    from app.features.analytics.schemas import ProblemShiftOut
366	    return [
367	        ProblemShiftOut(
368	            prod_date=r.d,
369	            shift=int(r.s),
370	            station_name=r.st,
371	            avg_oee=float(r.avg_oee) if r.avg_oee is not None else None,
372	            rejected_count=int(r.rejected_count or 0),
373	            total_production=int(r.p or 0),
374	            record_count=int(r.cnt or 0),
375	        ).model_dump()
376	        for r in rows
377	    ]
378

/** TanStack Query key fabrikası — tutarlı cache invalidation için tek kaynak. */
export const queryKeys = {
  imports: {
    all: ["imports"] as const,
    summary: (id: number) => ["imports", id, "summary"] as const,
    batches: ["imports", "batches"] as const,
    activeBatch: ["imports", "batches", "active"] as const,
  },
  records: {
    all: ["records"] as const,
    list: (filters: unknown) => ["records", "list", filters] as const,
    detail: (id: number) => ["records", id] as const,
  },
  validation: {
    issues: (filters?: unknown) => ["validation", "issues", filters] as const,
    summary: ["validation", "summary"] as const,
  },

    kpis: (filters?: unknown) => ["analytics", "kpis", filters] as const,
    oeeTrend: (filters?: unknown) => ["analytics", "oee-trend", filters] as const,
    shiftComparison: (filters?: unknown) => ["analytics", "shift-comparison", filters] as const,
    stationRanking: (filters?: unknown) => ["analytics", "station-ranking", filters] as const,
    qualityDistribution: (filters?: unknown) =>
      ["analytics", "quality-distribution", filters] as const,
    recentRecords: (batchId: number | null) =>
      ["analytics", "recent-records", batchId ?? "all"] as const,
    topStations: (batchId: number | null) =>
      ["analytics", "top-stations", batchId ?? "all"] as const,
    problemShifts: (batchId: number | null) =>
      ["analytics", "problem-shifts", batchId ?? "all"] as const,

export * from "./client";

## Kullanıcı

1	/**
2	 * Tek tip API client (native fetch). Tüm FastAPI çağrıları buradan geçer.
3	 * Hata sözleşmesi: { error: { code, message, detail } } → ApiError'a çevrilir.
4	 */
5	import { env } from "@/lib/env";
6	
7	export class ApiError extends Error {
8	  constructor(
9	    public readonly status: number,
10	    message: string,
11	    public readonly code?: string,
12	    public readonly detail?: unknown,
13	  ) {
14	    super(message);
15	    this.name = "ApiError";
16	  }
17	}
18	
19	type RequestOptions = Omit<RequestInit, "body"> & { body?: unknown };
20	
21	async function apiFetch<T>(path: string, options: RequestOptions = {}): Promise<T> {
22	  const { body, headers, ...rest } = options;
23	  const isForm = typeof FormData !== "undefined" && body instanceof FormData;
24	
25	  const res = await fetch(`${env.apiUrl}${path}`, {
26	    ...rest,
27	    headers: isForm ? headers : { "Content-Type": "application/json", ...headers },
28	    body: body === undefined ? undefined : isForm ? (body as FormData) : JSON.stringify(body),
29	  });
30	
31	  const isJson = res.headers.get("content-type")?.includes("application/json");
32	  const data = isJson ? await res.json() : await res.text();
33	
34	  if (!res.ok) {
35	    const err = (data as { error?: { code?: string; message?: string; detail?: unknown } })?.error;
36	    throw new ApiError(res.status, err?.message ?? res.statusText, err?.code, err?.detail ?? data);
37	  }
38	  return data as T;
39	}
40	
41	/**
42	 * Multipart yükleme — gerçek yükleme ilerlemesi (%) ile (XMLHttpRequest).
43	 * fetch upload progress'i desteklemediği için XHR kullanılır.
44	 * onProgress: 0–100 (yalnız yükleme fazı; sunucu işleme fazında 100'de bekler).
45	 */
46	function uploadWithProgress<T>(
47	  path: string,
48	  form: FormData,
49	  onProgress?: (percent: number) => void,
50	): Promise<T> {
51	  return new Promise<T>((resolve, reject) => {
52	    const xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
53	    xhr.open("POST", `${env.apiUrl}${path}`);
54	    xhr.responseType = "text";
55	
56	    xhr.upload.onprogress = (e) => {
57	      if (onProgress && e.lengthComputable) {
58	        onProgress(Math.round((e.loaded / e.total) * 100));
59	      }
60	    };
61	
62	    xhr.onload = () => {
63	      const ct = xhr.getResponseHeader("content-type") ?? "";
64	      const isJson = ct.includes("application/json");
65	      const data = isJson && xhr.responseText ? JSON.parse(xhr.responseText) : xhr.responseText;
66	      if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 300) {
67	        resolve(data as T);
68	      } else {
69	        const err = (data as { error?: { code?: string; message?: string; detail?: unknown } })
70	          ?.error;
71	        reject(
72	          new ApiError(xhr.status, err?.message ?? xhr.statusText, err?.code, err?.detail ?? data),
73	        );
74	      }
75	    };
76	    xhr.onerror = () => reject(new ApiError(0, "Ağ hatası (yükleme başarısız)"));
77	    xhr.send(form);
78	  });
79	}
80	
81	export const api = {
82	  get: <T>(path: string) => apiFetch<T>(path),
83	  post: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "POST", body }),
84	  patch: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "PATCH", body }),
85	  delete: <T = void>(path: string) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "DELETE" }),
86	  /** Multipart CSV yükleme — Content-Type'ı tarayıcı (boundary ile) ayarlar. */
87	  upload: <T>(path: string, form: FormData) => apiFetch<T>(path, { method: "POST", body: form }),
88	  /** İlerleme (%) raporlayan multipart yükleme. */
89	  uploadWithProgress,
90	};
91

## Kullanıcı

1	"use client";
2	
3	import * as React from "react";
4	import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
5	
6	export interface TabsContextValue {
7	  value: string;
8	  setValue: (v: string) => void;
9	}
10	
11	const TabsCtx = React.createContext<TabsContextValue | null>(null);
12	
13	function useTabs(): TabsContextValue {
14	  const ctx = React.useContext(TabsCtx);
15	  if (!ctx) throw new Error("Tabs bileşenleri <Tabs> içinde olmalı");
16	  return ctx;
17	}
18	
19	export interface TabsProps {
20	  value: string;
21	  onValueChange: (v: string) => void;
22	  children: React.ReactNode;
23	  className?: string;
24	}
25	
26	export function Tabs({ value, onValueChange, children, className }: TabsProps) {
27	  return (
28	    <TabsCtx.Provider value={{ value, setValue: onValueChange }}>
29	      <div className={className}>{children}</div>
30	    </TabsCtx.Provider>
31	  );
32	}
33	
34	export function TabsList({ className, children }: { className?: string; children: React.ReactNode }) {
35	  return (
36	    <div
37	      role="tablist"
38	      className={cn(
39	        "inline-flex h-9 items-center justify-center rounded-md bg-muted p-1 text-muted-foreground",
40	        className,
41	      )}
42	    >
43	      {children}
44	    </div>
45	  );
46	}
47	
48	export function TabsTrigger({
49	  value,
50	  children,
51	}: {
52	  value: string;
53	  children: React.ReactNode;
54	}) {
55	  const ctx = useTabs();
56	  const active = ctx.value === value;
57	  return (
58	    <button
59	      type="button"
60	      role="tab"
61	      aria-selected={active}
62	      onClick={() => ctx.setValue(value)}
63	      className={cn(
64	        "inline-flex items-center justify-center whitespace-nowrap rounded-sm px-3 py-1 text-sm font-medium transition-all",
65	        active
66	          ? "bg-background text-foreground shadow-sm"
67	          : "text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground",
68	      )}
69	    >
70	      {children}
71	    </button>
72	  );
73	}
74	
75	export function TabsContent({
76	  value,
77	  children,
78	  className,
79	}: {
80	  value: string;
81	  children: React.ReactNode;
82	  className?: string;
83	}) {
84	  const ctx = useTabs();
85	  if (ctx.value !== value) return null;
86	  return <div className={cn("mt-3", className)}>{children}</div>;
87	}

/**
 * Ortam değişkenleri erişimi (tek nokta).
 * NEXT_PUBLIC_* tarayıcıya gömülür → burada ASLA secret olmaz (hedef API key sadece backend).
 */
export const env = {
  /**
   * FastAPI backend base URL.
   * Varsayılan boş → same-origin: client "/api/v1/..." çağırır, Next rewrite
   * (next.config.mjs) bunu FastAPI'ye proxy'ler (CORS gerekmez, sıfır-config).
   * Doğrudan bağlanmak için NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=http://localhost:8000 set et.
   */
  apiUrl: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || "",
} as const;

23	@router.post("/run")
24	def run(
25	    record_ids: list[int] | None = None,
26	    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
27	) -> dict[str, object]:
28	    results = run_validation(db, record_ids=record_ids)
29	    db.commit()
30	    return {"summary": summarize(results), "record_count": len(results)}
31

33	@router.get("/summary")
34	def summary(db: Session = Depends(get_db)) -> dict[str, object]:
35	    results = run_validation(db)
36	    db.commit()
37	    return summarize(results)

40	@router.get("/issues")
41	def issues(
42	    category: IssueCategory | None = None,
43	    severity: IssueSeverity | None = None,
44	    rule_id: str | None = None,
45	    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
46	) -> list[dict[str, object]]:
47	    rows = db.execute(
48	        select(models.ValidationIssue).order_by(models.ValidationIssue.id.desc())
49	    ).scalars().all()
50	    out: list[dict[str, object]] = []
51	    for r in rows:
52	        if category is not None and r.category != category:
53	            continue
54	        if severity is not None and r.severity != severity:
55	            continue
56	        if rule_id is not None and r.rule_id != rule_id:
57	            continue
58	        out.append(
59	            {
60	                "id": r.id,
61	                "record_id": r.record_id,
62	                "rule_id": r.rule_id,
63	                "category": r.category,
64	                "severity": r.severity,
65	                "fields": r.field_names,
66	                "message": r.message,
67	                "suggested_action": r.suggested_action,
68	                "detected_at": r.detected_at.isoformat() if r.detected_at else None,
69	                "fixed_at": r.fixed_at.isoformat() if r.fixed_at else None,
70	                "status": r.status,
71	            }
72	        )
73	    return out
74	
75	
76	@router.get("/report")
77	def report(db: Session = Depends(get_db)) -> dict[str, object]:
78	    results = run_validation(db)
79	    db.commit()
80	    return full_report(results)

83	def _record_or_404(db: Session, record_id: int) -> models.ProductionRecord:
84	    rec = db.get(models.ProductionRecord, record_id)
85	    if rec is None:
86	        raise NotFoundError(f"Record {record_id} bulunamadı.")
87	    return rec
88	
89	
90	def _to_dict(rec: models.ProductionRecord) -> dict[str, object]:
91	    return {c.name: getattr(rec, c.name) for c in rec.__table__.columns}
92	
93	
94	@router.post("/records/{record_id}/fix")
95	def fix_record(
96	    record_id: int,
97	    patch: dict[str, object],
98	    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
99	) -> dict[str, object]:
100	    rec = _record_or_404(db, record_id)
101	    before = _to_dict(rec)
102	    for k, v in patch.items():
103	        if hasattr(rec, k):
104	            setattr(rec, k, v)
105	    rec.status = "valid"
106	    db.add(
107	        models.RecordEdit(
108	            record_id=rec.id,
109	            field="status",
110	            old_value=json.dumps(before, default=str, ensure_ascii=False),
111	            new_value=json.dumps(_to_dict(rec), default=str, ensure_ascii=False),
112	            reason="manual_fix",
113	            edited_by="operator",
114	        )
115	    )
116	    db.flush()
117	    return {"record_id": rec.id, "status": rec.status}
118	
119	
120	@router.post("/records/{record_id}/reject")
121	def reject_record(
122	    record_id: int,
123	    payload: dict[str, object] | None = None,
124	    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
125	) -> dict[str, object]:
126	    rec = _record_or_404(db, record_id)
127	    reason_in = (payload or {}).get("reason")
128	    before = _to_dict(rec)
129	    rec.status = "rejected"
130	    db.add(
131	        models.RecordEdit(
132	            record_id=rec.id,
133	            field="status",
134	            old_value=json.dumps(before, default=str, ensure_ascii=False),
135	            new_value=json.dumps(_to_dict(rec), default=str, ensure_ascii=False),
136	            reason=f"reject:{reason_in}" if reason_in else "reject",
137	            edited_by="operator",
138	        )
139	    )
140	    db.flush()
141	    return {"record_id": rec.id, "status": rec.status}
142	
143

145	def accept_record(

147	    payload: dict[str, object] | None = None,
148	    db: Session = Depends(get_db),

169	def list_edits(
170	    record_id: int,
171	    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
172	) -> list[dict[str, object]]:
173	    rec = _record_or_404(db, record_id)
174	    rows = db.execute(
175	        select(models.RecordEdit)
176	        .where(models.RecordEdit.record_id == rec.id)
177	        .order_by(models.RecordEdit.edited_at.desc())
178	    ).scalars().all()
179	    return [
180	        {
181	            "id": r.id,
182	            "field": r.field,
183	            "old_value": r.old_value,
184	            "new_value": r.new_value,
185	            "reason": r.reason,
186	            "edited_by": r.edited_by,
187	            "edited_at": r.edited_at.isoformat() if r.edited_at else None,
188	        }
189	        for r in rows
190	    ]

1	"""Validation engine — iki geçişli (row + batch) değerlendirme."""
2	from __future__ import annotations
3	
4	import math
5	from collections import Counter
6	from collections.abc import Sequence
7	from typing import Any
8	
9	from sqlalchemy import select
10	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
11	
12	from app.core.config import settings
13	from app.db import models
14	from app.features.validation.models import (
15	    Issue,
16	    IssueCategory,
17	    IssueSeverity,
18	    RuleContext,
19	    SuggestedAction,
20	    ValidationResult,
21	)
22	from app.features.validation.rules.consistency import CONSISTENCY_RULES
23	from app.features.validation.rules.domain import DOMAIN_RULES
24	from app.features.validation.rules.duplicate import DUPLICATE_RULES
25	from app.features.validation.rules.format_ import FORMAT_RULES
26	from app.features.validation.rules.missing import MISSING_RULES
27	from app.features.validation.rules.range_ import RANGE_RULES
28	
29	ALL_RULES: tuple[Any, ...] = (
30	    *MISSING_RULES,
31	    *RANGE_RULES,
32	    *CONSISTENCY_RULES,
33	    *DUPLICATE_RULES,
34	    *FORMAT_RULES,
35	    *DOMAIN_RULES,
36	)
37	
38	
39	def _build_context(current_file_hash: str | None = None) -> RuleContext:
40	    return RuleContext(
41	        tolerance_pct=settings.validation_tolerance_pct,
42	        p_suspect_upper=settings.validation_p_suspect_upper,
43	        p_impossible_upper=settings.validation_p_impossible_upper,
44	        minutes_per_day=settings.validation_minutes_per_day,
45	        outlier_z_threshold=settings.validation_outlier_z_threshold,
46	        work_order_pattern=settings.validation_work_order_pattern,
47	        station_pattern=settings.validation_station_pattern,
48	        window_start=settings.validation_report_window_start,
49	        window_end=settings.validation_report_window_end,
50	    )
51	
52	
53	def _attach_ctx_dynamic(ctx: RuleContext, db: Session) -> RuleContext:
54	    ctx.row_hash_seen = set()
55	    ctx.record_id_seen = {}
56	    ctx.file_hash_seen = set(
57	        db.execute(select(models.ImportBatch.file_hash)).scalars().all()
58	    )
59	    ctx.current_file_hash = None
60	    return ctx
61	
62	
63	def _check_row(record: Any, ctx: RuleContext) -> list[Issue]:
64	    out: list[Issue] = []
65	    for rule in ALL_RULES:
66	        try:
67	            res = rule.check(record, ctx)
68	        except Exception:
69	            continue
70	        if res is None:
71	            continue
72	        if isinstance(res, list):
73	            out.extend(res)
74	        else:
75	            out.append(res)
76	    return out
77	
78	
79	def _zscore_outliers(values: list[int], threshold: float) -> set[int]:
80	    if len(values) < 5:
81	        return set()
82	    mean = sum(values) / len(values)
83	    var = sum((v - mean) ** 2 for v in values) / len(values)
84	    std = math.sqrt(var) if var > 0 else 0.0
85	    if std == 0.0:
86	        return set()
87	    flagged: set[int] = set()
88	    for v in values:
89	        if abs((v - mean) / std) > threshold:
90	            flagged.add(int(v))
91	    return flagged
92	
93	
94	def _check_vd02_business_conflict(db: Session) -> dict[int, list[int]]:
95	    rows = db.execute(
96	        select(
97	            models.ProductionRecord.id,
98	            models.ProductionRecord.prod_date,
99	            models.ProductionRecord.shift,
100	            models.ProductionRecord.station_name,
101	            models.ProductionRecord.work_order_no,
102	            models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty,
103	            models.ProductionRecord.scrap_qty,
104	            models.ProductionRecord.oee,
105	        )
106	    ).all()
107	    bucket: dict[tuple[Any, Any, Any, Any], list[int]] = {}
108	    for r in rows:
109	        key = (r.prod_date, r.shift, r.station_name, r.work_order_no)
110	        bucket.setdefault(key, []).append(r[0])
111	    conflicts: dict[int, list[int]] = {}
112	    for key, ids in bucket.items():
113	        if len(ids) < 2:
114	            continue
115	        rows_in_key = [
116	            next(rr for rr in rows if rr[0] == rid) for rid in ids
117	        ]
118	        metrics: set[tuple[Any, ...]] = {
119	            (rr.produced_qty, rr.scrap_qty, rr.oee) for rr in rows_in_key
120	        }
121	        if len(metrics) > 1:
122	            for rid in ids:
123	                conflicts.setdefault(rid, []).extend(
124	                    [i for i in ids if i != rid]
125	                )
126	    return conflicts
127	
128	
129	def _build_record_proxy(model: models.ProductionRecord) -> Any:
130	    proxy = type("R", (), {})()
131	    for col in (
132	        "id",
133	        "record_id_src",
134	        "prod_date",
135	        "work_order_no",
136	        "work_center_no",
137	        "work_center_name",
138	        "station_name",
139	        "stock_name",
140	        "shift",
141	        "availability",
142	        "performance",
143	        "quality",
144	        "oee",
145	        "run_time",
146	        "down_time",
147	        "planned_down",
148	        "unplanned_down",
149	        "produced_qty",
150	        "scrap_qty",
151	        "row_hash",
152	        "status",
153	    ):
154	        setattr(proxy, col, getattr(model, col))
155	    return proxy
156	
157	
158	def _vd05_outlier_flag(db: Session, ctx: RuleContext) -> dict[int, str]:
159	    rows = db.execute(
160	        select(
161	            models.ProductionRecord.id,
162	            models.ProductionRecord.produced_qty,
163	        )
164	    ).all()
165	    flagged: dict[int, str] = {}
166	    values = [int(r.produced_qty) for r in rows if r.produced_qty is not None]
167	    outliers = _zscore_outliers(values, ctx.outlier_z_threshold)
168	    for rid, pq in rows:
169	        if pq is not None and int(pq) in outliers:
170	            flagged[int(rid)] = (
171	                f"Üretim miktarı ({int(pq)}) istatistiksel outlier "
172	                f"|z|>={ctx.outlier_z_threshold}."
173	            )
174	    return flagged
175	
176	
177	def _resolve_issues(
178	    results: dict[int, ValidationResult],
179	    conflict_map: dict[int, list[int]],
180	    outlier_map: dict[int, str],
181	) -> None:
182	    for rid, msg in outlier_map.items():
183	        results.setdefault(rid, ValidationResult(record_id=rid)).add(
184	            Issue(
185	                rule_id="V-X05",
186	                category=IssueCategory.DOMAIN,
187	                severity=IssueSeverity.WARNING,
188	                fields=("produced_qty",),
189	                message=msg,
190	                suggested_action=SuggestedAction.WARN,
191	            )
192	        )
193	    for rid, others in conflict_map.items():
194	        results.setdefault(rid, ValidationResult(record_id=rid)).add(
195	            Issue(
196	                rule_id="V-D02",
197	                category=IssueCategory.DUPLICATE,
198	                severity=IssueSeverity.WARNING,
199	                fields=("prod_date", "shift", "station_name", "work_order_no"),
200	                message=f"Çelişen kayıt(lar) var: ids={others}.",
201	                suggested_action=SuggestedAction.WARN,
202	            )
203	        )
204	
205	
206	def run_validation(
207	    db: Session,
208	    record_ids: Sequence[int] | None = None,
209	    current_file_hash: str | None = None,
210	) -> dict[int, ValidationResult]:
211	    ctx = _build_context(current_file_hash=current_file_hash)
212	    _attach_ctx_dynamic(ctx, db)
213	
214	    if record_ids is None:
215	        models_iter = db.execute(select(models.ProductionRecord)).scalars().all()
216	    else:
217	        models_iter = db.execute(
218	            select(models.ProductionRecord).where(
219	                models.ProductionRecord.id.in_(record_ids)
220	            )
221	        ).scalars().all()
222	
223	    results: dict[int, ValidationResult] = {}
224	    for m in models_iter:
225	        proxy = _build_record_proxy(m)
226	        issues = _check_row(proxy, ctx)
227	        res = ValidationResult(record_id=m.id)
228	        res.extend(issues)
229	        results[m.id] = res
230	
231	    conflict_map = _check_vd02_business_conflict(db)
232	    outlier_map = _vd05_outlier_flag(db, ctx)
233	    _resolve_issues(results, conflict_map, outlier_map)
234	
235	    for m in models_iter:
236	        status = results[m.id].status
237	        m.status = status.value
238	    db.flush()
239	    return results
240	
241	
242	def summarize(results: dict[int, ValidationResult]) -> dict[str, Any]:
243	    by_category: Counter[str] = Counter()
244	    by_severity: Counter[str] = Counter()
245	    by_rule: Counter[str] = Counter()
246	    by_status: Counter[str] = Counter()
247	    for r in results.values():
248	        by_status[r.status.value] += 1
249	        for i in r.issues:
250	            by_category[i.category.value] += 1
251	            by_severity[i.severity.value] += 1
252	            by_rule[i.rule_id] += 1
253	    return {
254	        "total_records": len(results),
255	        "by_status": dict(by_status),
256	        "by_category": dict(by_category),
257	        "by_severity": dict(by_severity),
258	        "by_rule": dict(by_rule),
259	    }
260

## Asistan

Confirmed: `run_validation` only persists record `status`, never writes to `validation_issues`. So `/issues` always returns `[]`. Let me read the Issue model, report.py, and the frontend validation types to build the correct fix.

## Kullanıcı

1	"""Validation domain modelleri — Enum + Issue + record status türetme."""
2	from __future__ import annotations
3	
4	from collections.abc import Sequence
5	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
6	from enum import StrEnum
7	
8	
9	class IssueCategory(StrEnum):
10	    MISSING = "missing"
11	    RANGE = "range"
12	    CONSISTENCY = "consistency"
13	    DUPLICATE = "duplicate"
14	    FORMAT = "format"
15	    DOMAIN = "domain"
16	
17	
18	class IssueSeverity(StrEnum):
19	    ERROR = "error"
20	    WARNING = "warning"
21	    INFO = "info"
22	
23	
24	class SuggestedAction(StrEnum):
25	    REJECT = "reject"
26	    WARN = "warn"
27	    FIX = "fix"
28	
29	
30	class RecordStatus(StrEnum):
31	    VALID = "valid"
32	    SUSPECT = "suspect"
33	    REJECTED = "rejected"
34	
35	
36	@dataclass(frozen=True)
37	class Issue:
38	    rule_id: str
39	    category: IssueCategory
40	    severity: IssueSeverity
41	    fields: tuple[str, ...]
42	    message: str
43	    suggested_action: SuggestedAction
44	
45	
46	@dataclass
47	class RuleContext:
48	    tolerance_pct: float
49	    p_suspect_upper: float
50	    p_impossible_upper: float
51	    minutes_per_day: int
52	    outlier_z_threshold: float
53	    work_order_pattern: str
54	    station_pattern: str
55	    window_start: str
56	    window_end: str
57	
58	
59	@dataclass
60	class ValidationResult:
61	    record_id: int
62	    issues: list[Issue] = field(default_factory=list)
63	
64	    def add(self, issue: Issue) -> None:
65	        self.issues.append(issue)
66	
67	    def extend(self, issues: Sequence[Issue]) -> None:
68	        self.issues.extend(issues)
69	
70	    @property
71	    def has_error(self) -> bool:
72	        return any(i.severity == IssueSeverity.ERROR for i in self.issues)
73	
74	    @property
75	    def has_warning(self) -> bool:
76	        return any(i.severity == IssueSeverity.WARNING for i in self.issues)
77	
78	    @property
79	    def status(self) -> RecordStatus:
80	        if self.has_error:
81	            return RecordStatus.REJECTED
82	        if self.has_warning:
83	            return RecordStatus.SUSPECT
84	        return RecordStatus.VALID
85

## Kullanıcı

1	"use client";
2	
3	import { useMutation, useQuery, useQueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
4	import { api } from "@/lib/api";
5	import { queryKeys } from "@/lib/query-keys";
6	import type { IssueFilter, RecordEdit, ValidationIssue, ValidationSummary } from "./types";
7	
8	export function useIssues(filter: IssueFilter) {
9	  const p = new URLSearchParams();
10	  if (filter.category) p.set("category", filter.category);
11	  if (filter.severity) p.set("severity", filter.severity);
12	  if (filter.rule_id) p.set("rule_id", filter.rule_id);
13	  const q = p.toString();
14	  return useQuery({
15	    queryKey: [...queryKeys.validation.issues(filter), q] as const,
16	    queryFn: () => api.get<ValidationIssue[]>(`/api/v1/validation/issues${q ? `?${q}` : ""}`),
17	  });
18	}
19	
20	export function useValidationSummary() {
21	  return useQuery({
22	    queryKey: queryKeys.validation.summary,
23	    queryFn: () => api.get<ValidationSummary>("/api/v1/validation/summary"),
24	  });
25	}
26	
27	export function useRecordEdits(recordId: number) {
28	  return useQuery({
29	    queryKey: queryKeys.records.detail(recordId),
30	    queryFn: () => api.get<RecordEdit[]>(`/api/v1/validation/records/${recordId}/edits`),
31	    enabled: recordId > 0,
32	  });
33	}
34	
35	export interface FixPayload {
36	  patch: Record<string, unknown>;
37	}
38	
39	export function useFixRecord() {
40	  const qc = useQueryClient();
41	  return useMutation({
42	    mutationFn: ({ recordId, patch }: { recordId: number; patch: Record<string, unknown> }) =>
43	      api.post<{ record_id: number; status: string }>(
44	        `/api/v1/validation/records/${recordId}/fix`,
45	        patch,
46	      ),
47	    onSuccess: () => {
48	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.issues({}) });
49	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.summary });
50	    },
51	  });
52	}
53	
54	export function useRejectRecord() {
55	  const qc = useQueryClient();
56	  return useMutation({
57	    mutationFn: ({ recordId, reason }: { recordId: number; reason?: string }) =>
58	      api.post<{ record_id: number; status: string }>(
59	        `/api/v1/validation/records/${recordId}/reject`,
60	        { reason: reason ?? null },
61	      ),
62	    onSuccess: () => {
63	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.issues({}) });
64	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.summary });
65	    },
66	  });
67	}
68	
69	export function useAcceptRecord() {
70	  const qc = useQueryClient();
71	  return useMutation({
72	    mutationFn: ({ recordId, reason }: { recordId: number; reason?: string }) =>
73	      api.post<{ record_id: number; status: string }>(
74	        `/api/v1/validation/records/${recordId}/accept`,
75	        { reason: reason ?? null },
76	      ),
77	    onSuccess: () => {
78	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.issues({}) });
79	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.summary });
80	    },
81	  });
82	}
83	
84	export function useRunValidation() {
85	  const qc = useQueryClient();
86	  return useMutation({
87	    mutationFn: () => api.post<{ record_count: number }>("/api/v1/validation/run"),
88	    onSuccess: () => {
89	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.summary });
90	      qc.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.validation.issues({}) });
91	    },
92	  });
93	}

Now let me read report.py to see if there's already an issue-flattening helper to reuse.

## Kullanıcı

1	"""Validation report — kategori/severity dağılımı + sistemik vs tekil tespiti."""
2	from __future__ import annotations
3	
4	from collections import Counter
5	from typing import Any
6	
7	from app.core.config import settings
8	from app.features.validation.models import (
9	    Issue,
10	    ValidationResult,
11	)
12	
13	
14	def category_breakdown(results: dict[int, ValidationResult]) -> dict[str, int]:
15	    c: Counter[str] = Counter()
16	    for r in results.values():
17	        for i in r.issues:
18	            c[i.category.value] += 1
19	    return dict(c)
20	
21	
22	def severity_breakdown(results: dict[int, ValidationResult]) -> dict[str, int]:
23	    s: Counter[str] = Counter()
24	    for r in results.values():
25	        for i in r.issues:
26	            s[i.severity.value] += 1
27	    return dict(s)
28	
29	
30	def rule_breakdown(results: dict[int, ValidationResult]) -> dict[str, int]:
31	    r: Counter[str] = Counter()
32	    for res in results.values():
33	        for i in res.issues:
34	            r[i.rule_id] += 1
35	    return dict(r)
36	
37	
38	def systemic_vs_unique(
39	    results: dict[int, ValidationResult],
40	    threshold_ratio: float | None = None,
41	) -> dict[str, list[str]]:
42	    if threshold_ratio is None:
43	        threshold_ratio = settings.validation_systemic_ratio
44	    total = max(len(results), 1)
45	    rb = rule_breakdown(results)
46	    systemic: list[str] = []
47	    unique: list[str] = []
48	    for rule_id, count in rb.items():
49	        if (count / total) >= threshold_ratio:
50	            systemic.append(rule_id)
51	        else:
52	            unique.append(rule_id)
53	    return {"systemic": sorted(systemic), "unique": sorted(unique)}
54	
55	
56	def issue_to_dict(issue: Issue) -> dict[str, Any]:
57	    return {
58	        "rule_id": issue.rule_id,
59	        "category": issue.category.value,
60	        "severity": issue.severity.value,
61	        "fields": list(issue.fields),
62	        "message": issue.message,
63	        "suggested_action": issue.suggested_action.value,
64	    }
65	
66	
67	def record_payload(record_id: int, result: ValidationResult) -> dict[str, Any]:
68	    return {
69	        "record_id": record_id,
70	        "issues": [issue_to_dict(i) for i in result.issues],
71	        "record_status": result.status.value,
72	    }
73	
74	
75	def full_report(results: dict[int, ValidationResult]) -> dict[str, Any]:
76	    return {
77	        "summary": {
78	            "total_records": len(results),
79	            "by_category": category_breakdown(results),
80	            "by_severity": severity_breakdown(results),
81	            "by_rule": rule_breakdown(results),
82	        },
83	        "systemic_vs_unique": systemic_vs_unique(results),
84	        "records": [record_payload(rid, r) for rid, r in results.items()],
85	    }
86

1	"use client";
2	
3	import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
4	import { useReactTable, getCoreRowModel, getSortedRowModel, flexRender, type ColumnDef, type SortingState } from "@tanstack/react-table";
5	import { Badge, severityTone } from "@/components/ui/badge";
6	import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
7	import { useIssues } from "./useValidation";
8	import type { ValidationIssue } from "./types";
9	
10	export interface IssueListProps {
11	  recordStatus?: string;
12	  onSelect: (issue: ValidationIssue) => void;
13	}
14	
15	export function IssueList({ recordStatus, onSelect }: IssueListProps) {
16	  const filter = useMemo(() => ({ record_status: recordStatus }), [recordStatus]);
17	  const issues = useIssues(filter);
18	  const [sorting, setSorting] = useState<SortingState>([]);
19	
20	  const columns = useMemo<ColumnDef<ValidationIssue>[]>(
21	    () => [
22	      {
23	        accessorKey: "record_id",
24	        header: "Record",
25	        cell: (info) => <span className="font-mono text-xs">#{info.getValue<number>()}</span>,
26	      },
27	      {
28	        accessorKey: "rule_id",
29	        header: "Kural",
30	        cell: (info) => <span className="font-mono text-xs">{info.getValue<string>()}</span>,
31	      },
32	      {
33	        accessorKey: "severity",
34	        header: "Seviye",
35	        cell: (info) => {
36	          const s = info.getValue<string>();
37	          return <Badge tone={severityTone(s)}>{s}</Badge>;
38	        },
39	      },
40	      {
41	        accessorKey: "category",
42	        header: "Kategori",
43	        cell: (info) => <Badge tone="outline">{info.getValue<string>()}</Badge>,
44	      },
45	      {
46	        accessorKey: "fields",
47	        header: "Alan(lar)",
48	        cell: (info) => (
49	          <span className="font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">
50	            {info.getValue<string | null>() ?? "—"}
51	          </span>
52	        ),
53	      },
54	      {
55	        accessorKey: "message",
56	        header: "Mesaj",
57	        cell: (info) => <span className="line-clamp-2">{info.getValue<string>()}</span>,
58	      },
59	      {
60	        accessorKey: "suggested_action",
61	        header: "Aksiyon",
62	        cell: (info) => <Badge tone="outline">{info.getValue<string>()}</Badge>,
63	      },
64	    ],
65	    [],
66	  );
67	
68	  const table = useReactTable({
69	    data: issues.data ?? [],
70	    columns,
71	    state: { sorting },
72	    onSortingChange: setSorting,
73	    getCoreRowModel: getCoreRowModel(),
74	    getSortedRowModel: getSortedRowModel(),
75	  });
76	
77	  return (
78	    <div className="rounded-lg border bg-card text-card-foreground">
79	      <table className="w-full text-sm">
80	        <thead>
81	          {table.getHeaderGroups().map((hg) => (
82	            <tr key={hg.id} className="border-b text-left text-muted-foreground">
83	              {hg.headers.map((h) => (
84	                <th
85	                  key={h.id}
86	                  className="cursor-pointer p-2 select-none"
87	                  onClick={h.column.getToggleSortingHandler()}
88	                >
89	                  {flexRender(h.column.columnDef.header, h.getContext())}
90	                  {h.column.getIsSorted() === "asc" ? " ▲" : h.column.getIsSorted() === "desc" ? " ▼" : ""}
91	                </th>
92	              ))}
93	            </tr>
94	          ))}
95	        </thead>
96	        <tbody>
97	          {issues.isLoading ? (
98	            Array.from({ length: 6 }).map((_, i) => (
99	              <tr key={`s_${i}`} className="border-b">
100	                <td colSpan={columns.length} className="p-2">
101	                  <Skeleton className="h-6 w-full" />
102	                </td>
103	              </tr>
104	            ))
105	          ) : table.getRowModel().rows.length === 0 ? (
106	            <tr>
107	              <td colSpan={columns.length} className="p-4 text-center text-muted-foreground">
108	                Bu sekmede issue yok.
109	              </td>
110	            </tr>
111	          ) : (
112	            table.getRowModel().rows.map((row) => (
113	              <tr
114	                key={row.id}
115	                className="cursor-pointer border-b hover:bg-muted/50"
116	                onClick={() => onSelect(row.original)}
117	              >
118	                {row.getVisibleCells().map((cell) => (
119	                  <td key={cell.id} className="p-2 align-top">
120	                    {flexRender(cell.column.columnDef.cell, cell.getContext())}
121	                  </td>
122	                ))}
123	              </tr>
124	            ))
125	          )}
126	        </tbody>
127	      </table>
128	    </div>
129	  );
130	}

1	"use client";
2	
3	import { useState } from "react";
4	import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";

13	
14	export function ValidationPage() {
15	  const [tab, setTab] = useState("all");
16	  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<ValidationIssue | null>(null);
17	  const summary = useValidationSummary();
18	  const run = useRunValidation();

22	    tab === "suspect" ? "suspect" : tab === "rejected" ? "rejected" : undefined;

31	        }),

34	    });

41	          <p className="font-mono text-sm text-muted-foreground">MAGNA · Validasyon</p>
42	          <h1 className="mt-1 text-3xl font-bold tracking-tight">Validation Issues</h1>
43	        </div>
44	        <Button onClick={onRun} disabled={run.isPending}>
45	          {run.isPending ? "Çalışıyor…" : "Tüm kayıtları doğrula"}
46	        </Button>
47	      </header>
48	
49	      <section className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 md:grid-cols-4">

51	          label="Toplam"

53	          tone="default"

55	        />

59	          tone="success"
60	          loading={summary.isLoading}
61	        />
62	        <SummaryCard
63	          label="Suspect"
64	          value={summary.data?.by_status?.suspect ?? null}
65	          tone="warning"
66	          loading={summary.isLoading}

69	          label="Rejected"

71	          tone="destructive"
72	          loading={summary.isLoading}
73	        />
74	      </section>

77	        <TabsList>
78	          <TabsTrigger value="all">Tümü</TabsTrigger>
79	          <TabsTrigger value="suspect">Şüpheli</TabsTrigger>
80	          <TabsTrigger value="rejected">Reddedildi</TabsTrigger>
81	        </TabsList>
82	        <TabsContent value="all">
83	          <IssueList onSelect={setSelected} />
84	        </TabsContent>
85	        <TabsContent value="suspect">
86	          <IssueList recordStatus="suspect" onSelect={setSelected} />
87	        </TabsContent>
88	        <TabsContent value="rejected">
89	          <IssueList recordStatus="rejected" onSelect={setSelected} />
90	        </TabsContent>
91	      </Tabs>
92	
93	      <IssueDetailDrawer issue={selected} onClose={() => setSelected(null)} />
94	    </main>
95	  );
96	}
97	
98	function SummaryCard({
99	  label,
100	  value,
101	  tone,
102	  loading,
103	}: {
104	  label: string;
105	  value: number | null;
106	  tone: "default" | "success" | "warning" | "destructive";
107	  loading?: boolean;
108	}) {
109	  const toneText: Record<typeof tone, string> = {
110	    default: "text-foreground",
111	    success: "text-oee-good",
112	    warning: "text-oee-mid",
113	    destructive: "text-oee-low",
114	  };
115	  return (
116	    <Card>
117	      <CardHeader>
118	        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground">{label}</CardTitle>
119	      </CardHeader>
120	      <CardContent>
121	        {loading ? (
122	          <Skeleton className="h-7 w-20" />
123	        ) : (
124	          <p className={`text-2xl font-semibold tabular-nums ${toneText[tone]}`}>
125	            {value ?? 0}
126	          </p>
127	        )}
128	      </CardContent>
129	    </Card>
130	  );
131	}

1	"use client";
2	
3	import { useState } from "react";
4	import { useSubmitSync, useSyncPreview } from "./useSync";
5	import type { SyncGroupPreview } from "./types";
6	
7	const SHIFT_LABELS: Record<number, string> = { 1: "Sabah", 2: "Öğle", 3: "Gece" };
8	
9	function fmt(n: number): string {
10	  return new Intl.NumberFormat("tr-TR").format(n);
11	}
12	
13	export function SyncPage() {
14	  const preview = useSyncPreview();
15	  const submit = useSubmitSync();
16	  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
17	  const [force, setForce] = useState(false);
18	
19	  const toggle = (key: string) => {
20	    setSelected((prev) => {
21	      const next = new Set(prev);
22	      if (next.has(key)) next.delete(key);
23	      else next.add(key);
24	      return next;
25	    });
26	  };
27	
28	  const selectAll = () => {
29	    if (!preview.data) return;
30	    setSelected(new Set(preview.data.groups.map((g) => g.idempotency_key)));
31	  };
32	
33	  const clearAll = () => setSelected(new Set());
34	
35	  const onSubmit = () => {
36	    const groups = preview.data?.groups ?? [];
37	    const targets: Array<{ production_date: string; shift: number }> = [];
38	    for (const key of selected) {
39	      const g = groups.find((x) => x.idempotency_key === key);
40	      if (g) targets.push({ production_date: g.production_date, shift: g.shift });
41	    }
42	    if (targets.length === 1) {
43	      submit.mutate({
44	        production_date: targets[0].production_date,
45	        shift: targets[0].shift,
46	        force,
47	      });
48	    } else {
49	      submit.mutate({ force });
50	    }
51	  };
52	
53	  return (
54	    <main className="container mx-auto py-8">
55	      <header className="mb-6 flex items-end justify-between">
56	        <div>
57	          <p className="font-mono text-sm text-muted-foreground">MAGNA · Hedef API Senkronizasyonu</p>
58	          <h1 className="mt-1 text-3xl font-bold tracking-tight">Sync</h1>
59	          <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
60	            Sadece <span className="text-oee-good">valid</span> kayıtlar (gün, vardiya) agrege edilerek
61	            gönderilir. Hatalı kayıt <strong>asla</strong> gitmez.
62	          </p>
63	        </div>
64	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
65	          <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
66	            <input type="checkbox" checked={force} onChange={(e) => setForce(e.target.checked)} />
67	            Force (hash değiştiyse yeni submission)
68	          </label>
69	          <button
70	            type="button"
71	            className="rounded-md border bg-background px-3 py-1 text-sm text-foreground"
72	            onClick={selectAll}
73	          >
74	            Tümünü seç
75	          </button>
76	          <button
77	            type="button"
78	            className="rounded-md border bg-background px-3 py-1 text-sm text-foreground"
79	            onClick={clearAll}
80	          >
81	            Temizle
82	          </button>
83	          <button
84	            type="button"
85	            disabled={selected.size === 0 || submit.isPending}
86	            onClick={onSubmit}
87	            className="rounded-md bg-primary px-4 py-1.5 text-sm font-medium text-primary-foreground disabled:opacity-50"
88	          >
89	            {submit.isPending ? "Gönderiliyor…" : `Gönder (${selected.size})`}
90	          </button>
91	        </div>
92	      </header>
93	
94	      {submit.data ? (
95	        <section className="mb-4 rounded-lg border bg-card p-4 text-sm text-card-foreground">
96	          <div>
97	            <strong>Kabul:</strong> {submit.data.accepted.length} ·{" "}
98	            <strong>Zaten başarılı:</strong> {submit.data.skipped_already_success.length} ·{" "}
99	            <strong>Hash çakışması:</strong> {submit.data.rejected_due_to_hash_conflict.length}
100	          </div>
101	        </section>
102	      ) : null}
103	
104	      <section className="rounded-lg border bg-card text-card-foreground">
105	        <table className="w-full text-sm">
106	          <thead>
107	            <tr className="border-b text-left text-muted-foreground">
108	              <th className="p-2"></th>
109	              <th className="p-2">Tarih</th>
110	              <th className="p-2">Vardiya</th>
111	              <th className="p-2 text-right">Makine</th>
112	              <th className="p-2 text-right">Üretim</th>
113	              <th className="p-2 text-right">OEE</th>
114	              <th className="p-2 text-right">Kayıt</th>
115	              <th className="p-2">Idempotency</th>
116	            </tr>
117	          </thead>
118	          <tbody>
119	            {preview.isLoading ? (
120	              <tr>
121	                <td colSpan={8} className="p-4 text-center text-muted-foreground">
122	                  Yükleniyor…
123	                </td>
124	              </tr>
125	            ) : (preview.data?.groups ?? []).length === 0 ? (
126	              <tr>
127	                <td colSpan={8} className="p-4 text-center text-muted-foreground">
128	                  Gönderilecek geçerli kayıt yok. Önce import + validation çalıştırın.
129	                </td>
130	              </tr>
131	            ) : (
132	              (preview.data?.groups ?? []).map((g) => (
133	                <PreviewRow
134	                  key={g.idempotency_key}
135	                  group={g}
136	                  selected={selected.has(g.idempotency_key)}
137	                  onToggle={() => toggle(g.idempotency_key)}
138	                />
139	              ))
140	            )}
141	          </tbody>
142	        </table>
143	      </section>
144	    </main>
145	  );
146	}

148	function PreviewRow({
149	  group,

151	  onToggle,
152	}: {

154	  selected: boolean;
155	  onToggle: () => void;
156	}) {
157	  return (
158	    <tr className="border-b hover:bg-muted/50">

161	      </td>

165	      <td className="p-2 text-right tabular-nums">{fmt(group.total_production_units)}</td>
166	      <td className="p-2 text-right tabular-nums">
167	        {group.oe_value === null ? "—" : `${group.oe_value.toFixed(1)}%`}
168	      </td>
169	      <td className="p-2 text-right tabular-nums">{fmt(group.source_record_count)}</td>
170	      <td className="p-2 font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground">{group.idempotency_key}</td>
171	    </tr>
172	  );
173	}
